    13	// ErrorType returns an [attribute.KeyValue] identifying the error type of err.
    14	//
    15	// If err is nil, the returned attribute has the default value
    16	// [ErrorTypeOther].
    17	//
    18	// If err or one of the errors in its chain has the method
    19	//
    20	//      ErrorType() string
    21	//
    22	// the returned attribute has that method's return value. If multiple errors in
    23	// the chain implement this method, the value from the first match found by
    24	// [errors.As] is used. Otherwise, the returned attribute has a value derived
    25	// from the concrete type of err.
    26	//
    27	// The key of the returned attribute is [ErrorTypeKey].
    28	func ErrorType(err error) attribute.KeyValue {
    29	        if err == nil {
    30	                return ErrorTypeOther
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        return ErrorTypeKey.String(errorType(err))
    34	}
    35	
    36	func errorType(err error) string {
    37	        var s string
    38	        if et, ok := err.(interface{ ErrorType() string }); ok {
    39	                // Fast path: check the top-level error first.
    40	                s = et.ErrorType()
    41	        } else {
    42	                // Fallback: search the error chain for an ErrorType method.
    43	                var et interface{ ErrorType() string }
    44	                if errors.As(err, &et) {
    45	                        // Prioritize the ErrorType method if available.
    46	                        s = et.ErrorType()
    47	                }
    48	        }
    49	        if s == "" {
    50	                // Fallback to reflection if the ErrorType method is not supported or
    51	                // returns an empty value.
    52	
    53	                t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
    54	                pkg, name := t.PkgPath(), t.Name()
    55	                if pkg != "" && name != "" {
    56	                        s = pkg + "." + name
    57	                } else {
    58	                        // The type has no package path or name (predeclared, not-defined,
    59	                        // or alias for a not-defined type).
    60	                        //
    61	                        // This is not guaranteed to be unique, but is a best effort.
    62	                        s = t.String()

=== semconv/v1.34.0/error_type.go
// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.34.0"

import (
	"fmt"
	"reflect"

	"go.opentelemetry.io/otel/attribute"
)

// ErrorType returns an [attribute.KeyValue] identifying the error type of err.
func ErrorType(err error) attribute.KeyValue {
	if err == nil {
		return ErrorTypeOther
	}
	t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
	var value string
	if t.PkgPath() == "" && t.Name() == "" {
		// Likely a builtin type.
		value = t.String()
	} else {
		value = fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s", t.PkgPath(), t.Name())
	}

	if value == "" {
		return ErrorTypeOther
	}
	return ErrorTypeKey.String(value)
}

=== semconv/v1.37.0/error_type.go
// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.37.0"

import (
	"reflect"

	"go.opentelemetry.io/otel/attribute"
)

// ErrorType returns an [attribute.KeyValue] identifying the error type of err.
//
// If err is nil, the returned attribute has the default value
// [ErrorTypeOther].
//
// If err's type has the method
//
//	ErrorType() string
//
// then the returned attribute has the value of err.ErrorType(). Otherwise, the
// returned attribute has a value derived from the concrete type of err.
//
// The key of the returned attribute is [ErrorTypeKey].
func ErrorType(err error) attribute.KeyValue {
	if err == nil {
		return ErrorTypeOther
	}

	return ErrorTypeKey.String(errorType(err))
}

func errorType(err error) string {
	var s string
	if et, ok := err.(interface{ ErrorType() string }); ok {
		// Prioritize the ErrorType method if available.
		s = et.ErrorType()
	}
	if s == "" {
		// Fallback to reflection if the ErrorType method is not supported or
		// returns an empty value.

		t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
		pkg, name := t.PkgPath(), t.Name()
		if pkg != "" && name != "" {
			s = pkg + "." + name
		} else {
			// The type has no package path or name (predeclared, not-defined,
			// or alias for a not-defined type).
			//
			// This is not guaranteed to be unique, but is a best effort.
			s = t.String()
		}
	}
	return s
}

=== semconv/v1.40.0/error_type.go
// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.40.0"

import (
	"errors"
	"reflect"

	"go.opentelemetry.io/otel/attribute"
)

// ErrorType returns an [attribute.KeyValue] identifying the error type of err.
//
// If err is nil, the returned attribute has the default value
// [ErrorTypeOther].
//
// If err or one of the errors in its chain has the method
//
//	ErrorType() string
//
// the returned attribute has that method's return value. If multiple errors in
// the chain implement this method, the value from the first match found by
// [errors.As] is used. Otherwise, the returned attribute has a value derived
// from the concrete type of err.
//
// The key of the returned attribute is [ErrorTypeKey].
func ErrorType(err error) attribute.KeyValue {
	if err == nil {
		return ErrorTypeOther
	}

	return ErrorTypeKey.String(errorType(err))
}

func errorType(err error) string {
	var s string
	if et, ok := err.(interface{ ErrorType() string }); ok {
		// Fast path: check the top-level error first.
		s = et.ErrorType()
	} else {
		// Fallback: search the error chain for an ErrorType method.
		var et interface{ ErrorType() string }
		if errors.As(err, &et) {
			// Prioritize the ErrorType method if available.
			s = et.ErrorType()
		}
	}
	if s == "" {
		// Fallback to reflection if the ErrorType method is not supported or
		// returns an empty value.

		t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
		pkg, name := t.PkgPath(), t.Name()
		if pkg != "" && name != "" {
			s = pkg + "." + name
		} else {
			// The type has no package path or name (predeclared, not-defined,
			// or alias for a not-defined type).
			//
			// This is not guaranteed to be unique, but is a best effort.
			s = t.String()
		}
	}
	return s
}

semconv/v1.40.0/error_type_test.go
// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.40.0"

import (
	"errors"
	"testing"
)

const pkg = "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.40.0"

func TestErrorType(t *testing.T) {
	check(t, nil, ErrorTypeOther.Value.AsString())
	check(t, errors.New("msg"), "*errors.errorString")
	check(t, custom("aborted"), "aborted")
	check(t, errors.Join(custom("left"), custom("right")), "left") // first errors.As match is used.
	check(t, custom(""), pkg+".ErrCustomType")                     // empty ErrorType, use concrete type.
	check(t, wrapped(custom("wrapped-aborted")), "wrapped-aborted")
	check(t, wrapped(custom("")), pkg+".wrappedErr") // empty ErrorType in chain, use concrete top-level type.
}

func check(t *testing.T, err error, want string) {
	t.Helper()
	got := ErrorType(err)
	if got.Key != ErrorTypeKey {
		t.Errorf("ErrorType(%v) key = %v, want %v", err, got.Key, ErrorTypeKey)
	}
	if got.Value.AsString() != want {
		t.Errorf("ErrorType(%v) value = %v, want %v", err, got.Value.AsString(), want)
	}
}

func custom(typ string) error {
	return ErrCustomType{Type: typ}
}

func wrapped(err error) error {
	return wrappedErr{err: err}
}

type ErrCustomType struct {
	Type string
}

func (e ErrCustomType) Error() string {
	return "custom: " + e.Type
}

func (e ErrCustomType) ErrorType() string {
	return e.Type
}

type wrappedErr struct {
	err error
}

func (e wrappedErr) Error() string {
	return "wrapped: " + e.err.Error()
}

func (e wrappedErr) Unwrap() error {
	return e.err
}
semconv/v1.34.0/error_type_test.go
// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.34.0"

import (
	"errors"
	"fmt"
	"reflect"
	"testing"

	"go.opentelemetry.io/otel/attribute"
)

type CustomError struct{}

func (CustomError) Error() string {
	return "custom error"
}

func TestErrorType(t *testing.T) {
	customErr := CustomError{}
	builtinErr := errors.New("something went wrong")
	var nilErr error

	wantCustomType := reflect.TypeFor[CustomError]()
	wantCustomStr := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s", wantCustomType.PkgPath(), wantCustomType.Name())

	tests := []struct {
		name string
		err  error
		want attribute.KeyValue
	}{
		{
			name: "BuiltinError",
			err:  builtinErr,
			want: attribute.String("error.type", "*errors.errorString"),
		},
		{
			name: "CustomError",
			err:  customErr,
			want: attribute.String("error.type", wantCustomStr),
		},
		{
			name: "NilError",
			err:  nilErr,
			want: ErrorTypeOther,
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			got := ErrorType(tt.err)
			if got != tt.want {
				t.Errorf("ErrorType(%v) = %v, want %v", tt.err, got, tt.want)
			}
		})
	}
}

}

func (e ErrCustomType) Error() string {
	return "custom: " + e.Type
}

func (e ErrCustomType) ErrorType() string {
	return e.Type

semconv/v1.37.0/error_type_test.go
// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.37.0"

import (
	"errors"
	"testing"
)

const pkg = "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.37.0"

func TestErrorType(t *testing.T) {
	check(t, nil, ErrorTypeOther.Value.AsString())
	check(t, errors.New("msg"), "*errors.errorString")
	check(t, custom("aborted"), "aborted")
	check(t, custom(""), pkg+".ErrCustomType") // empty ErrorType, use concrete type.
}

func check(t *testing.T, err error, want string) {
	t.Helper()
	got := ErrorType(err)
	if got.Key != ErrorTypeKey {
		t.Errorf("ErrorType(%v) key = %v, want %v", err, got.Key, ErrorTypeKey)
	}
	if got.Value.AsString() != want {
		t.Errorf("ErrorType(%v) value = %v, want %v", err, got.Value.AsString(), want)
	}
}

func custom(typ string) error {
	return ErrCustomType{Type: typ}
}

type ErrCustomType struct {
	Type string
}

func (e ErrCustomType) Error() string {
	return "custom: " + e.Type
}

func (e ErrCustomType) ErrorType() string {
	return e.Type
}
semconv/v1.36.0/error_type_test.go
// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.36.0"

import (
	"errors"
	"fmt"
	"reflect"
	"testing"

	"go.opentelemetry.io/otel/attribute"
)

type CustomError struct{}

func (CustomError) Error() string {
	return "custom error"
}

func TestErrorType(t *testing.T) {
	customErr := CustomError{}
	builtinErr := errors.New("something went wrong")
	var nilErr error

	wantCustomType := reflect.TypeFor[CustomError]()
	wantCustomStr := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s", wantCustomType.PkgPath(), wantCustomType.Name())

	tests := []struct {
		name string
		err  error
		want attribute.KeyValue
	}{
		{
			name: "BuiltinError",
			err:  builtinErr,
			want: attribute.String("error.type", "*errors.errorString"),
		},
		{
			name: "CustomError",
			err:  customErr,
			want: attribute.String("error.type", wantCustomStr),
		},
		{
			name: "NilError",
			err:  nilErr,
			want: ErrorTypeOther,
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			got := ErrorType(tt.err)
			if got != tt.want {
				t.Errorf("ErrorType(%v) = %v, want %v", tt.err, got, tt.want)
			}
		})
	}
}

    13	// ErrorType returns an [attribute.KeyValue] identifying the error type of err.
    14	//
    15	// If err is nil, the returned attribute has the default value
    16	// [ErrorTypeOther].
    17	//
    18	// If err or one of the errors in its chain has the method
    19	//
    20	//      ErrorType() string
    21	//
    22	// the returned attribute has that method's return value. If multiple errors in
    23	// the chain implement this method, the value from the first match found by
    24	// [errors.As] is used. Otherwise, the returned attribute has a value derived
    25	// from the concrete type of err.
    26	//
    27	// The key of the returned attribute is [ErrorTypeKey].
    28	func ErrorType(err error) attribute.KeyValue {
    29	        if err == nil {
    30	                return ErrorTypeOther
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        return ErrorTypeKey.String(errorType(err))
    34	}
    35	
    36	func errorType(err error) string {
    37	        var s string
    38	        if et, ok := err.(interface{ ErrorType() string }); ok {
    39	                // Fast path: check the top-level error first.
    40	                s = et.ErrorType()
    41	        } else {
    42	                // Fallback: search the error chain for an ErrorType method.
    43	                var et interface{ ErrorType() string }
    44	                if errors.As(err, &et) {
    45	                        // Prioritize the ErrorType method if available.
    46	                        s = et.ErrorType()
    47	                }
    48	        }
    49	        if s == "" {
    50	                // Fallback to reflection if the ErrorType method is not supported or
    51	                // returns an empty value.
    52

    57	                } else {

    59	                        // or alias for a not-defined type).
    60	                        //
    61	                        // This is not guaranteed to be unique, but is a best effort.

// unwrapFmtError unwraps errors created by fmt.Errorf with a single %w.
//
// fmt'"'"'s wrapping error type only records context and otherwise obscures the
// user-defined error type. Unwrap these implementation details so error.type is
// derived from the outermost non-fmt wrapping error.
func unwrapFmtError(err error) error {
	for {
		if t := reflect.TypeOf(err); t == nil || t.PkgPath() != "fmt" || t.Name() != "wrapError" {
			return err
		}

		wrapped := errors.Unwrap(err)
		if wrapped == nil {
			return err
		}
		err = wrapped
	}
}' --insert_line 66

    69	// unwrapFmtError unwraps errors created by fmt.Errorf with a single %w.
    70	//
    71	// fmt's wrapping error type only records context and otherwise obscures the
    72	// user-defined error type. Unwrap these implementation details so error.type is
    73	// derived from the outermost non-fmt wrapping error.
    74	func unwrapFmtError(err error) error {
    75	        for {
    76	                if t := reflect.TypeOf(err); t == nil || t.PkgPath() != "fmt" || t.Name() != "wrapError" {
    77	                        return err
    78	                }
    79	
    80	                wrapped := errors.Unwrap(err)
    81	                if wrapped == nil {
    82	                        return err
    83	                }
    84	                err = wrapped
    85	        }
    86	}
    87	}

// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors

package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.40.0"

import (
	"errors"
	"reflect"

	"go.opentelemetry.io/otel/attribute"
)

// ErrorType returns an [attribute.KeyValue] identifying the error type of err.
//
// If err is nil, the returned attribute has the default value
// [ErrorTypeOther].
//
// If err or one of the errors in its chain has the method
//
//	ErrorType() string
//
// the returned attribute has that method's return value. If multiple errors in
// the chain implement this method, the value from the first match found by
// [errors.As] is used. Otherwise, the returned attribute has a value derived
// from the concrete type of err.
//
// The key of the returned attribute is [ErrorTypeKey].
func ErrorType(err error) attribute.KeyValue {
	if err == nil {
		return ErrorTypeOther
	}

	return ErrorTypeKey.String(errorType(err))
}

func errorType(err error) string {
	var s string
	if et, ok := err.(interface{ ErrorType() string }); ok {
		// Fast path: check the top-level error first.
		s = et.ErrorType()
	} else {
		// Fallback: search the error chain for an ErrorType method.
		var et interface{ ErrorType() string }
		if errors.As(err, &et) {
			// Prioritize the ErrorType method if available.
			s = et.ErrorType()
		}
	}
	if s == "" {
		// Fallback to reflection if the ErrorType method is not supported or
		// returns an empty value.
		err = unwrapFmtError(err)

		t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
		pkg, name := t.PkgPath(), t.Name()
		if pkg != "" && name != "" {
			s = pkg + "." + name
		} else {
			// The type has no package path or name (predeclared, not-defined,
			// or alias for a not-defined type).
			//
			// This is not guaranteed to be unique, but is a best effort.
			s = t.String()
		}
	}
	return s
}

// unwrapFmtError unwraps errors created by fmt.Errorf with a single %w.
//
// fmt's wrapping error type only records context and otherwise obscures the
// user-defined error type. Unwrap these implementation details so error.type is
// derived from the outermost non-fmt wrapping error.
func unwrapFmtError(err error) error {
	for {
		if t := reflect.TypeOf(err); t == nil || t.PkgPath() != "fmt" || t.Name() != "wrapError" {
			return err
		}

		wrapped := errors.Unwrap(err)
		if wrapped == nil {
			return err
		}
		err = wrapped
	}
}

     1	// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
     2	// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
     3	
     4	package semconv // import "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/{{.TagVer}}"
     5	
     6	import (
     7	        "errors"
     8	        "reflect"
     9	
    10	        "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/attribute"
    11	)
    12	
    13	// ErrorType returns an [attribute.KeyValue] identifying the error type of err.
    14	//
    15	// If err is nil, the returned attribute has the default value
    16	// [ErrorTypeOther].
    17	//
    18	// If err or one of the errors in its chain has the method
    19	//
    20	//      ErrorType() string
    21	//
    22	// the returned attribute has that method's return value. If multiple errors in
    23	// the chain implement this method, the value from the first match found by
    24	// [errors.As] is used. Otherwise, the returned attribute has a value derived
    25	// from the concrete type of err.
    26	//
    27	// The key of the returned attribute is [ErrorTypeKey].
    28	func ErrorType(err error) attribute.KeyValue {
    29	        if err == nil {
    30	                return ErrorTypeOther
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        return ErrorTypeKey.String(errorType(err))
    34	}
    35	
    36	func errorType(err error) string {
    37	        var s string
    38	        if et, ok := err.(interface{ ErrorType() string }); ok {
    39	                // Fast path: check the top-level error first.
    40	                s = et.ErrorType()
    41	        } else {
    42	                // Fallback: search the error chain for an ErrorType method.
    43	                var et interface{ ErrorType() string }
    44	                if errors.As(err, &et) {
    45	                        // Prioritize the ErrorType method if available.
    46	                        s = et.ErrorType()
    47	                }
    48	        }
    49	        if s == "" {
    50	                // Fallback to reflection if the ErrorType method is not supported or
    51	                // returns an empty value.
    52	                err = unwrapFmtError(err)
    53	
    54	                t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
    55	                pkg, name := t.PkgPath(), t.Name()
    56	                if pkg != "" && name != "" {
    57	                        s = pkg + "." + name
    58	                } else {
    59	                        // The type has no package path or name (predeclared, not-defined,
    60	                        // or alias for a not-defined type).
    61	                        //
    62	                        // This is not guaranteed to be unique, but is a best effort.
    63	                        s = t.String()
    64	                }
    65	        }
    66	        return s
    67	}
    68	
    69	// unwrapFmtError unwraps errors created by fmt.Errorf with a single %w.
    70	//
    71	// fmt's wrapping error type only records context and otherwise obscures the
    72	// user-defined error type. Unwrap these implementation details so error.type is
    73	// derived from the outermost non-fmt wrapping error.
    74	func unwrapFmtError(err error) error {
    75	        for {
    76	                if !isFmtWrapError(err) {
    77	                        return err
    78	                }
    79	
    80	                wrapped := errors.Unwrap(err)
    81	                if wrapped == nil {
    82	                        return err
    83	                }
    84	                err = wrapped
    85	        }
    86	}
    87	
    88	func isFmtWrapError(err error) bool {
    89	        t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
    90	        if t == nil {
    91	                return false
    92	        }
    93	        if t.Kind() == reflect.Pointer {
    94	                t = t.Elem()
    95	        }
    96	        return t.PkgPath() == "fmt" && t.Name() == "wrapError"
    97	}
    98

cat >/tmp/edge_error_type.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TMP=$(mktemp -d)
trap 'rm -rf "$TMP"' EXIT
cat >"$TMP/go.mod" <<'EOM'
module edge

go 1.23.0

require go.opentelemetry.io/otel v0.0.0

replace go.opentelemetry.io/otel => /testbed
EOM
cat >"$TMP/main.go" <<'EOM'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"

	semconv "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/semconv/v1.40.0"
)

type inner struct{}
func (inner) Error() string { return "inner" }

type outer struct{ err error }
func (o outer) Error() string { return o.err.Error() }
func (o outer) Unwrap() error { return o.err }

func check(name string, err error, want string) {
	got := semconv.ErrorType(err).Value.AsString()
	fmt.Printf("%s: got %q want %q\n", name, got, want)
	if got != want { os.Exit(1) }
}

func main() {
	check("fmt unwrap stops at custom wrapper", fmt.Errorf("ctx: %w", outer{inner{}}), "main.outer")
	check("multi wrap stays fmt", fmt.Errorf("ctx: %w %w", inner{}, outer{inner{}}), "*fmt.wrapErrors")
}
EOM
(cd "$TMP" && go mod tidy && go run .)
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/edge_error_type.sh
/tmp/edge_error_type.sh

 }
+
+// unwrapFmtError unwraps errors created by fmt.Errorf with a single %w.
+//
+// fmt's wrapping error type only records context and otherwise obscures the
+// user-defined error type. Unwrap these implementation details so error.type is
+// derived from the outermost non-fmt wrapping error.
+func unwrapFmtError(err error) error {
+	for {
+		if !isFmtWrapError(err) {
+			return err
+		}
+
+		wrapped := errors.Unwrap(err)
+		if wrapped == nil {
+			return err
+		}
+		err = wrapped
+	}
+}
+
+func isFmtWrapError(err error) bool {
+	t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
+	if t == nil {
+		return false
+	}
+	if t.Kind() == reflect.Pointer {
+		t = t.Elem()
+	}
+	return t.PkgPath() == "fmt" && t.Name() == "wrapError"
+}

+
+// unwrapFmtError unwraps errors created by fmt.Errorf with a single %w.
+//
+// fmt's wrapping error type only records context and otherwise obscures the
+// user-defined error type. Unwrap these implementation details so error.type is
+// derived from the outermost non-fmt wrapping error.
+func unwrapFmtError(err error) error {
+	for {
+		if !isFmtWrapError(err) {
+			return err
+		}
+
+		wrapped := errors.Unwrap(err)
+		if wrapped == nil {
+			return err
+		}
+		err = wrapped
+	}
+}
+
+func isFmtWrapError(err error) bool {
+	t := reflect.TypeOf(err)
+	if t == nil {
+		return false
+	}
+	if t.Kind() == reflect.Pointer {
+		t = t.Elem()
+	}
+	return t.PkgPath() == "fmt" && t.Name() == "wrapError"
+}
